                                    2126             +*/*   between an ERP and write-to- operator and                      */

                                    2134             +*/*         including the macro in a module.  The extension id       */
                                    2135             +*/*         must be initialized to IOSB, the length of the           */
                                    2136             +*/*         extension must be set, and flag IOSBEXTF must be set     */

                                    2748             +*/********************************************************************/
                                    2749             +*/* Notes on Bit Combinations                                        */
                                    2750             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    2751             +*/* IOSPSLL - 0 = local lock needed for IOS post status processing,  */
                                    2752             +*/*               the local lock is obtained and the local lock save */
                                    2753             +*/*               area is passed via register 13 to various exits.   */
                                    2754             +*/*           1 = local lock is not needed                           */
                                    2755             +*/* IOSIDR  - 1 = paging I/O therefore, ERPs must use indirect       */
                                    2756             +*/*               recording for requests, ie, the ERP sets IOSPROC to*/
                                    2757             +*/*               IOSWTO to have ERP messages scheduled.  Also,      */
                                    2758             +*/*               if ASM (IOSNOLL = 0), the address of a save area   */
                                    2759             +*/*               is passed via the ASM control block IORB.          */
                                    2760             +*/* IOSNOLL - 0 = the local lock may be obtained.                    */
                                    2761             +*/*           1 = the I/O driver has indicated that the local lock   */
                                    2762             +*/*               cannot be obtained.  The local lock may already be */
                                    2763             +*/*               owned in which case dead lock could occur.  Also,  */
                                    2764             +*/*               the local lock may not be owned, but the I/O driver*/
                                    2765             +*/*               has reasons for not wanting IECVPST to obtain it.  */
                                    2766             +*/*               Generally used by paging subsystems other than ASM */
                                    2767             +*/*               (for example, Media Manager) that are called by    */
                                    2768             +*/*               applications that could own the local lock but     */
                                    2769             +*/*               cannot pass a save area in an IORB.  IOSPSLL must  */
                                    2770             +*/*               also be on.  Post status gets the CPU lock, calls  */
                                    2771             +*/*               the IOS storage manager for a block of storage,    */
                                    2772             +*/*               frees the CPU lock and passes the IOS large block  */
                                    2773             +*/*               as a save area.  Performance should be considered  */
                                    2774             +*/*               when using this method.                        @19C*/

                                    2786             +*/* |        |        |         | save area.                        |*/

                                    2791             +*/* |   1    |    1   |    0    | I/O driver must use indirect      |*/
